41/// \brief Structure storing the transmission window timing parameters.
42struct du_tx_window_timing_parameters {
43 /// Offset from the current OTA symbol to the start of DL Control-Plane transmission window.
44 std::chrono::microseconds T1a_max_cp_dl;
45 /// Offset from the current OTA symbol to the end of DL Control-Plane transmission window.
46 std::chrono::microseconds T1a_min_cp_dl;
47 /// Offset from the current OTA symbol to the start of UL Control-Plane transmission window.
48 std::chrono::microseconds T1a_max_cp_ul;
49 /// Offset from the current OTA symbol to the end of UL Control-Plane transmission window.
50 std::chrono::microseconds T1a_min_cp_ul;
51 /// Offset from the current OTA symbol to the start of DL User-Plane transmission window.
52 std::chrono::microseconds T1a_max_up;
53 /// Offset from the current OTA symbol to the end of DL User-Plane transmission window.
54 std::chrono::microseconds T1a_min_up;
55};
56
57/// Configuration used by ofh_symbol_handler implementations.
58struct symbol_handler_config {
59 /// Transmission window timing parameters for delay management.
60 du_tx_window_timing_parameters tx_timing_params;
61 /// Number of symbols per slot.
62 unsigned symbols_per_slot;
63 /// Highest subcarrier spacing.
64 subcarrier_spacing scs;
65};
66
67/// Open Fronthaul transmitter configuration.
68struct transmitter_config {
69 /// Radio sector identifier.
70 unsigned sector;
71 /// Channel bandwidth.
72 bs_channel_bandwidth_fr1 bw;
73 /// Subcarrier spacing.
74 subcarrier_spacing scs;
75 /// Cyclic prefix.
76 cyclic_prefix cp;
77 /// Downlink eAxC.
78 static_vector<unsigned, MAX_NOF_SUPPORTED_EAXC> dl_eaxc;
79 /// Uplink eAxC.
80 static_vector<unsigned, MAX_NOF_SUPPORTED_EAXC> ul_eaxc;
81 /// PRACH eAxC.
82 static_vector<unsigned, MAX_NOF_SUPPORTED_EAXC> prach_eaxc;
83 /// PRACH Contol-Plane enabled flag.
84 bool is_prach_cp_enabled;
85 /// Destination MAC address.
86 ether::mac_address mac_dst_address;
87 /// Source MAC address.
88 ether::mac_address mac_src_address;
89 /// Tag control information field.
90 uint16_t tci;
91 /// Ethernet interface name or identifier.
92 std::string interface;
93 /// Promiscuous mode flag.
94 bool is_promiscuous_mode_enabled;
95 /// MTU size.
96 units::bytes mtu_size;
97 /// RU working bandwidth.
98 bs_channel_bandwidth_fr1 ru_working_bw;
99 /// Open Fronthaul symbol handler configuration.
100 symbol_handler_config symbol_handler_cfg;
101 /// Downlink compression parameters.
102 ru_compression_params dl_compr_params;
103 /// Uplink compression parameters.
104 ru_compression_params ul_compr_params;
105 /// PRACH compression parameters.
106 ru_compression_params prach_compr_params;
107 /// Downlink static compression header flag.
108 bool is_downlink_static_compr_hdr_enabled;
109 /// \brief Downlink broadcast flag.
110 ///
111 /// If this flag is enabled the same downlink data will be send to all the configured downlink eAxCs.
112 bool downlink_broadcast;
113 /// IQ samples scaling factor.
114 float iq_scaling;
115 /// Downlink processing time in microseconds.
116 std::chrono::microseconds dl_processing_time;
117 /// Optional TDD configuration.
118 optional<tdd_ul_dl_config_common> tdd_config;
119 /// Indicates if DPDK should be used by the underlying implementation.
120 bool uses_dpdk;
121};
122
